</td></tr>

<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Symphonies&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Symphonies</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For orchestra</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the orchestra</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Symphony No.9
</td></tr>

</th>

<td>E minor
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>4 movements:
<ol><li> Adagio—Allegro molto (E minor)
</li><li> Largo (D-flat major)
</li><li> Molto vivace (E minor)
</li><li> Allegro con fuoco (E major)
</li></ol>

</th>
